						newh =  (e.gh[ix] * m) + (e.tabh + e.thumbh);
					}
					var el = document.getElementById(e.c);
					if (el!==null && el) el.style.height = newh+"px";
					el = document.getElementById(e.c+"_wrapper");
					if (el!==null && el) {
						el.style.height = newh+"px";
						el.style.display = "block";
					}
				} catch(e){
					console.log("Failure at Presize of Slider:" + e)
				}
			//});
		  };</script>

        <script type="rocketlazyloadscript">
        (function(){
            if (!document.querySelector('.scroll-content-column') || !document.querySelector('.scroll-map-column')) return;
            window._mciMapInstances = window._mciMapInstances || {};
            var captured = false;
            var captureMap = function() {
                if (captured || typeof google === 'undefined' || !google.maps || !google.maps.Map) return;
                var Orig = google.maps.Map;
                google.maps.Map = function(div, opts) {
                    var m = new Orig(div, opts);
                    if (div && div.id) window._mciMapInstances[div.id] = m;
                    return m;
                };
                for (var k in Orig) if (Orig.hasOwnProperty(k)) google.maps.Map[k] = Orig[k];
                google.maps.Map.prototype = Orig.prototype;
                captured = true;
            };
            if (typeof google !== 'undefined' && google.maps && google.maps.Map) captureMap();
            else {
                var t = setInterval(function(){
                    if (typeof google !== 'undefined' && google.maps && google.maps.Map) {
                        captureMap();
                        clearInterval(t);
                    }
                }, 50);
                setTimeout(function(){ clearInterval(t); }, 10000);
            }
        })();
        </script>

        <script type="rocketlazyloadscript" data-rocket-type="text/javascript">
function fetch(){
    jQuery('.input_search').off('input').on('input', function() { // .off() removes any previous event listeners
	        // Check if the input field is empty
        if (jQuery(this).val().trim() === '') {
            // Clear the data display if no input
            jQuery('#datafetch').empty();
            return; // Exit if the input is empty
        }	
	jQuery(this).after('<img src="https://www.1000towns.ca/wp-content/uploads/2022/02/red-car-hover.gif" class="ms-cto-spinner" />');

 //   jQuery('.input_search').after('<img src="https://www.1000towns.ca/wp-content/uploads/2022/02/red-car-hover.gif" class="ms-cto-spinner" />');
   
		jQuery.ajax({
        url: 'https://1000towns.ca/wp-admin/admin-ajax.php',
        type: 'post',
        data: { action: 'data_fetch', keyword: jQuery('#keyword').val() },
        success: function(data) {
            jQuery('.ms-cto-spinner').remove();
            jQuery('#datafetch').html( data );
        }
    });
});
}
</script>

				const lazyloadRunObserver = () => {
					const lazyloadBackgrounds = document.querySelectorAll( `.e-con.e-parent:not(.e-lazyloaded)` );
					const lazyloadBackgroundObserver = new IntersectionObserver( ( entries ) => {
						entries.forEach( ( entry ) => {
							if ( entry.isIntersecting ) {
								let lazyloadBackground = entry.target;
								if( lazyloadBackground ) {
									lazyloadBackground.classList.add( 'e-lazyloaded' );
								}
								lazyloadBackgroundObserver.unobserve( entry.target );
							}
						});
					}, { rootMargin: '200px 0px 200px 0px' } );
					lazyloadBackgrounds.forEach( ( lazyloadBackground ) => {
						lazyloadBackgroundObserver.observe( lazyloadBackground );
					} );
				};
				const events = [
					'DOMContentLoaded',
					'elementor/lazyload/observe',
				];
				events.forEach( ( event ) => {
					document.addEventListener( event, lazyloadRunObserver );
				} );
			</script>
